2330
2338[[nodiscard]] constexpr std::optional<char32_t> ucd_get_composition(char32_t cp1, char32_t cp2) noexcept
2339{
2340 constexpr auto max_code_point_hi = detail::ucd_compositions_indices_size - 1;
2341
2342 auto code_point_hi = cp1 / detail::ucd_compositions_chunk_size;
2343 hilet code_point_lo = cp1 % detail::ucd_compositions_chunk_size;
2344
2345 if (code_point_hi > max_code_point_hi) {
2346 code_point_hi = max_code_point_hi;
2347 }
2348
2349 // The index in the chunk-index table based on the upper-bits of the code-point.
2350 hilet chunk_index = load_bits_be<detail::ucd_compositions_index_width>(
2351 detail::ucd_compositions_indices_bytes,
2352 code_point_hi * detail::ucd_compositions_index_width);
2353
2354 // Add back in the lower-bits of the code-point.
2355 hilet index = (chunk_index * detail::ucd_compositions_chunk_size) + code_point_lo;
2356
2357 // Get the composition value from the composition table by index.
2358 hilet value = load_bits_be<detail::ucd_composition_width>(
2359 detail::ucd_compositions_bytes, index * detail::ucd_composition_width);
2360
2361 constexpr auto cp_size_width = 5;
2362 constexpr auto cp_size_mask = (1_uz << cp_size_width) - 1;
2363 hilet cp_size = value & cp_size_mask;
2364 if (cp_size == 0) {
2365 return std::nullopt;
2366 }
2367
2368 hilet cp_index = value >> cp_size_width;
2369
2370 auto offset = cp_index * 2_uz * detail::ucd_compositions_code_point_width;
2371 for (auto i = 0_uz; i != cp_size; ++i, offset += detail::ucd_compositions_code_point_width) {
2372 hilet second_cp = load_bits_be<detail::ucd_compositions_code_point_width>(
2373 detail::ucd_composition_code_points_bytes, offset);
2374
2375 if (second_cp == cp2) {
2376 offset += cp_size * detail::ucd_compositions_code_point_width;
2377
2378 hilet result_cp = load_bits_be<detail::ucd_compositions_code_point_width>(
2379 detail::ucd_composition_code_points_bytes, offset);
2380
2381 return char_cast<char32_t>(result_cp);
2382
2383 } else if (second_cp > cp2) {
2384 // Early out, `load_bits_be` is kinda expensive and on average (mean)
2385 // this list is about 15 entries in size.
2386 return std::nullopt;
2387 }
2388 }
2389
2390 return std::nullopt;
2391}
